             </h2>
             <div class="tensorsite-content__description">
              <p>
               TensorFlow is an end-to-end open source platform for machine learning. It has a comprehensive, flexible ecosystem of tools, libraries and community resources that lets researchers push the state-of-the-art in ML and developers easily build and deploy ML powered applications.
              </p>

            <div class="tensorsite-content">
             <h2 class="tensorsite-content__title tensorsite-content__title--grow" data-text="       Build, deploy, and experiment easily with TensorFlow     " id="build,-deploy,-and-experiment-easily-with-tensorflow">
              Build, deploy, and experiment easily with TensorFlow
